# <a name="supported-metrics-with-azure-monitor"></a><span data-ttu-id="dab13-103">支援 Azure 監視器的計量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dab13-103">Supported metrics with Azure Monitor</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="dab13-104">Azure 監視器提供數種與計量進行互動的方式，包括在入口網站中製作計量圖表、透過 REST API 存取計量，或使用 PowerShell 或 CLI 查詢計量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dab13-104">Azure Monitor provides several ways to interact with metrics, including charting them in the portal, accessing them through the REST API, or querying them using PowerShell or CLI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dab13-105">以下是目前可供 Azure 監視器計量管線使用的所有計量完整清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dab13-105">Below is a complete list of all metrics currently available with Azure Monitor's metric pipeline.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="dab13-106">其他計量可在入口網站中或使用舊版 API 提供。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dab13-106">Other metrics may be available in the portal or using legacy APIs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dab13-107">這份清單僅包含使用彙總 Azure 監視器計量管線的公開預覽時可供使用的公開預覽計量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dab13-107">This list only includes public preview metrics available using the public preview of the consolidated Azure Monitor metric pipeline.</span></span>
>
>
